Npt_GuideLine.img
  NptGuide
    Text00 = "- Introduction \r\n "
    Text01 = "This system is designed to enable users to make transactions with game items using Nexon Cash."
    Text02 = "This system will ensure that both parties will make safe & secured transactions. \r\n\r\n"
    Text03 = "- [For Sale] \r\n "
    Text04 = "1. Selling an item : \r\n"
    Text05 = "Select the item to sell in the inventory at the bottom-left corner of the screen, and press Sell/Auction , then it'll be registered under the [For Sale] list."
    Text06 = "When the item is registered, a registration fee (mesos) will be charged."
    Text07 = "Please be aware that even if the item is later removed from the list, the registration fee will NOT be returned."
    Text08 = "Also, once the item is listed under  "For Sale", the item is deleted from your inventory,"
    Text09 = "and will not be available for use in the game. In order to use the item, remove the item from the For Sale list. \r\n\r\n"
    Text10 = "2. Purchasing an item on sale：\r\n "
    Text11 = "You may purchase the item by simply clicking [Wanted] on the item you'd like to buy."
    Text12 = "Please check all the details on the item (item name, unit, price, option, etc.) before making the purchase. \r\n\r\n"
    Text13 = "3. Transaction Fee : \r\n "
    Text14 = "Once the item is registered for sale, the transaction fee of [500 Nexon Cash + 7% of the item price] will be added to the listed price."
    Text15 = "After the item is sold, the difference between the registered price and the actual selling price will be construed as the transaction fee. "
    Text16 = "The fee will be given to the user that buys the item. \r\n\r\n"
    Text17 = "4. Cart：\r\n "
    Text18 = "If there are multiple items to purchase, you may store the items in the Shopping Cart,"
    Text19 = "The items stored in the shopping cart can be seen through the Cart button at My Page. \r\n\r\n"
    Text20 = "- [Wanted] \r\n "
    Text21 = "1. Add to Cart：\r\n "
    Text22 = "By clicking on this button, you can register an item you'd like to buy under [Wanted], and purchase the selected item owned by other users. \r\n\r\n"
    Text23 = "2. Transaction fee：\r\n "
    Text24 = "Once the item is added to the cart, the transaction fee of [500 Nexon Cash + 7% of the item price] will be added to the listed price."
    Text25 = "After the item is bought, the difference between the registered price and the actual selling price will be construed as the transaction fee."
    Text26 = "The price of purchase will be listed, minus the transaction fee. \r\n\r\n"
    Text27 = "- [My Page] \r\n "
    Text28 = "1. Cart：\r\n "
    Text29 = "You can see all the items in the cart, as well as items you've reserved, all in this list."
    Text30 = "The cart will not be emptied out the moment you log out of the game. \r\n\r\n"
    Text31 = "2. Reserved Item \r\n"
    Text32 = "You can see the list of items that have been reserved."
    Text33 = "If the item is up on the market by a user, you may head directly to that page and make the purchase. \r\n\r\n"
    Text34 = "3. History : \r\n"
    Text35 = "This is where you can check your history of transaction on MTS. \r\n\r\n"
    Text36 = "4. Auction Progress : \r\n"
    Text37 = "This is the place to check up on your progress in the auction. \r\n\r\n"
    Text38 = "- Others \r\n"
    Text39 = "Editing the Registered Information：\r\n"
    Text40 = "Once the item has been registered for sale or to buy, the information cannot be edited."
    Text41 = "To do so, please cancel the registration and re-register. \r\n\r\n"
